            - generic [ref=e216]:
              - heading "Locator" [level=1] [ref=e218]
              - paragraph [ref=e219]:
                - text: Locators are the central piece of Playwright's auto-waiting and retry-ability. In a nutshell, locators represent a way to find element(s) on the page at any moment. A locator can be created with the
                - link "page.locator()" [ref=e220] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-locator
                - text: method.
              - paragraph [ref=e221]:
                - link "Learn more about locators" [ref=e222] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/locators
                - text: .
              - separator [ref=e223]
              - heading "MethodsDirect link to Methods" [level=2] [ref=e224]:
                - text: Methods
                - link "Direct link to Methods" [ref=e225] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#methods"
                  - text: "#"
              - heading "allDirect link to all" [level=3] [ref=e226]:
                - text: all
                - link "Direct link to all" [ref=e227] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#locator-all"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.29"
              - paragraph [ref=e228]: When the locator points to a list of elements, this returns an array of locators, pointing to their respective elements.
              - generic [ref=e229]:
                - generic [ref=e230]:
                  - img [ref=e232]
                  - text: note
                - generic [ref=e234]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e235]:
                    - link "locator.all()" [ref=e236] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-all
                    - text: does not wait for elements to match the locator, and instead immediately returns whatever is present in the page.
                  - paragraph [ref=e237]:
                    - text: When the list of elements changes dynamically,
                    - link "locator.all()" [ref=e238] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-all
                    - text: will produce unpredictable and flaky results.
                  - paragraph [ref=e239]:
                    - text: When the list of elements is stable, but loaded dynamically, wait for the full list to finish loading before calling
                    - link "locator.all()" [ref=e240] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-all
                    - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e241]:
                - strong [ref=e242]: Usage

              - paragraph [ref=e420]:
                - strong [ref=e421]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e422]: This method captures the aria snapshot of the given element. The snapshot is a string that represents the state of the element and its children. The snapshot can be used to assert the state of the element in the test, or to compare it to state in the future.
              - paragraph [ref=e423]:
                - text: The ARIA snapshot is represented using
                - link "YAML" [ref=e424] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://yaml.org/spec/1.2.2/
                - text: "markup language:"
              - list [ref=e425]:
                - listitem [ref=e426]: The keys of the objects are the roles and optional accessible names of the elements.
                - listitem [ref=e427]: The values are either text content or an array of child elements.
                - listitem [ref=e428]:
                  - text: Generic static text can be represented with the
                  - code [ref=e429]: text
                  - text: key.

              - paragraph [ref=e677]:
                - strong [ref=e678]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e679]: "Performs the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e680]:
                - listitem [ref=e681]: Ensure that element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws. If the element is already checked, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e682]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e683] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e684] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-check-option-force
                  - text: option is set.
                - listitem [ref=e685]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e686]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e687] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e688]: Ensure that the element is now checked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e689]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e690]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e691] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-check-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e692] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

              - paragraph [ref=e762]:
                - text: This method waits for
                - link "actionability" [ref=e763] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/actionability
                - text: checks, focuses the element, clears it and triggers an
                - code [ref=e764]: input
                - text: event after clearing.
              - paragraph [ref=e765]:
                - text: If the target element is not an
                - code [ref=e766]: <input>
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e767]: <textarea>
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e768]: "[contenteditable]"
                - text: element, this method throws an error. However, if the element is inside the
                - code [ref=e769]: <label>
                - text: element that has an associated
                - link "control" [ref=e770] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLLabelElement/control
                - text: ", the control will be cleared instead."

              - paragraph [ref=e926]:
                - strong [ref=e927]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e928]: "This method clicks the element by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e929]:
                - listitem [ref=e930]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e931] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e932] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-click-option-force
                  - text: option is set.
                - listitem [ref=e933]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e934]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e935] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element, or the specified
                  - link "position" [ref=e936] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-click-option-position
                  - text: .
                - listitem [ref=e937]:
                  - text: Wait for initiated navigations to either succeed or fail, unless
                  - link "noWaitAfter" [ref=e938] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-click-option-no-wait-after
                  - text: option is set.
              - paragraph [ref=e939]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e940]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e941] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-click-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e942] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-dblclick-option-force
                  - text: option is set.
                - listitem [ref=e1145]: Scroll the element into view if needed.

                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e1147] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse

                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-dblclick-option-position
                  - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e1149]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e1150]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e1151] [cursor=pointer]:

                - code [ref=e1297]: composed
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e1298]: cancelable
                - text: and bubble by default.

              - paragraph [ref=e1767]:
                - text: This method waits for
                - link "actionability" [ref=e1768] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/actionability
                - text: checks, focuses the element, fills it and triggers an
                - code [ref=e1769]: input
                - text: event after filling. Note that you can pass an empty string to clear the input field.
              - paragraph [ref=e1770]:
                - text: If the target element is not an
                - code [ref=e1771]: <input>
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e1772]: <textarea>
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e1773]: "[contenteditable]"
                - text: element, this method throws an error. However, if the element is inside the
                - code [ref=e1774]: <label>
                - text: element that has an associated
                - link "control" [ref=e1775] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLLabelElement/control
                - text: ", the control will be filled instead."

                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.22"
              - paragraph [ref=e1781]: This method narrows existing locator according to the options, for example filters by text. It can be chained to filter multiple times.
              - paragraph [ref=e1782]:
                - strong [ref=e1783]: Usage
              - generic [ref=e1785]:
                - code [ref=e1787]:
                  - generic [ref=e1788]: const rowLocator = page.locator('tr');
                  - generic [ref=e1789]: // ...
                  - generic [ref=e1790]: await rowLocator
                  - generic [ref=e1791]: ".filter({ hasText: 'text in column 1' })"
                  - generic [ref=e1792]: ".filter({ has: page.getByRole('button', { name: 'column 2 button' }) })"
                  - generic [ref=e1793]: .screenshot();
                - generic [ref=e1794]:
                  - button "Toggle word wrap" [ref=e1795] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - img [ref=e1796]
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e1798] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e1799]:
                      - img [ref=e1800]
                      - img [ref=e1802]
              - paragraph [ref=e1804]:
                - strong [ref=e1805]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e1806]:
                - listitem [ref=e1807]:
                  - code [ref=e1808]: options
                  - link "Object" [ref=e1809] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                  - emphasis [ref=e1810]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e1811]:
                    - listitem [ref=e1812]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e1813]:
                        - code [ref=e1814]: has
                        - link "Locator" [ref=e1815] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                        - emphasis [ref=e1816]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e1817] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-filter-option-has"
                      - paragraph [ref=e1818]:
                        - text: Narrows down the results of the method to those which contain elements matching this relative locator. For example,
                        - code [ref=e1819]: article
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e1820]: text=Playwright
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e1821]: <article><div>Playwright</div></article>
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e1822]:
                        - text: Inner locator
                        - strong [ref=e1823]: must be relative
                        - text: to the outer locator and is queried starting with the outer locator match, not the document root. For example, you can find
                        - code [ref=e1824]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e1825]: div
                        - text: in
                        - code [ref=e1826]: <article><content><div>Playwright</div></content></article>
                        - text: . However, looking for
                        - code [ref=e1827]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e1828]: article div
                        - text: will fail, because the inner locator must be relative and should not use any elements outside the
                        - code [ref=e1829]: content
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e1830]:
                        - text: Note that outer and inner locators must belong to the same frame. Inner locator must not contain
                        - link "FrameLocator" [ref=e1831] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-framelocator
                        - text: s.
                    - listitem [ref=e1832]:

                        - text: that does not have

                        - text: matches

              - paragraph [ref=e2408]:
                - strong [ref=e2409]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e2410]:
                - text: Role selector
                - strong [ref=e2411]: does not replace
                - text: accessibility audits and conformance tests, but rather gives early feedback about the ARIA guidelines.
              - paragraph [ref=e2412]:
                - text: Many html elements have an implicitly
                - link "defined role" [ref=e2413] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://w3c.github.io/html-aam/#html-element-role-mappings
                - text: that is recognized by the role selector. You can find all the
                - link "supported roles here" [ref=e2414] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-1.2/#role_definitions
                - text: . ARIA guidelines
                - strong [ref=e2415]: do not recommend
                - text: duplicating implicit roles and attributes by setting
                - code [ref=e2416]: role
                - text: and/or
                - code [ref=e2417]: aria-*
                - text: attributes to default values.

              - paragraph [ref=e2492]: Allows locating elements that contain given text.
              - paragraph [ref=e2493]:
                - text: See also
                - link "locator.filter()" [ref=e2494] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-filter
                - text: that allows to match by another criteria, like an accessible role, and then filter by the text content.

              - paragraph [ref=e2497]: "Consider the following DOM structure:"

              - generic [ref=e2513]:
                - code [ref=e2515]:
                  - generic [ref=e2516]: // Matches <span>
                  - generic [ref=e2517]: page.getByText('world');
                  - generic [ref=e2518]: // Matches first <div>
                  - generic [ref=e2519]: page.getByText('Hello world');
                  - generic [ref=e2520]: // Matches second <div>
                  - generic [ref=e2521]: "page.getByText('Hello', { exact: true });"
                  - generic [ref=e2522]: // Matches both <div>s
                  - generic [ref=e2523]: page.getByText(/Hello/);
                  - generic [ref=e2524]: // Matches second <div>
                  - generic [ref=e2525]: page.getByText(/^hello$/i);
                - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e2527] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - generic [ref=e2528]:

                      - paragraph [ref=e2555]: "Whether to find an exact match: case-sensitive and whole-string. Default to false. Ignored when locating by a regular expression. Note that exact match still trims whitespace."
              - paragraph [ref=e2556]:
                - strong [ref=e2557]: Returns
              - list [ref=e2558]:
                - listitem [ref=e2559]:
                  - link "Locator" [ref=e2560] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - link "#" [ref=e2561] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#locator-get-by-text-return"
              - paragraph [ref=e2562]:
                - strong [ref=e2563]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e2564]: Matching by text always normalizes whitespace, even with exact match. For example, it turns multiple spaces into one, turns line breaks into spaces and ignores leading and trailing whitespace.
              - paragraph [ref=e2565]:
                - text: Input elements of the type
                - code [ref=e2566]: button
                - text: and
                - code [ref=e2567]: submit
                - text: are matched by their
                - code [ref=e2568]: value
                - text: instead of the text content. For example, locating by text
                - code [ref=e2569]: "\"Log in\""
                - text: matches
                - code [ref=e2570]: <input type=button value="Log in">
                - text: .
              - separator [ref=e2571]
              - heading "getByTitleDirect link to getByTitle" [level=3] [ref=e2572]:
                - text: getByTitle
                - link "Direct link to getByTitle" [ref=e2573] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#locator-get-by-title"

                  - text: option is set.

                  - text: Use

                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse

                  - link "position" [ref=e2769] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-hover-option-position
                  - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e2770]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e2771]:

                  - paragraph [ref=e3328]: A selector or locator to use when resolving DOM element.
                - listitem [ref=e3329]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e3330]:
                    - code [ref=e3331]: options
                    - link "Object" [ref=e3332] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                    - emphasis [ref=e3333]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e3334]:
                    - listitem [ref=e3335]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e3336]:
                        - code [ref=e3337]: has
                        - link "Locator" [ref=e3338] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                        - emphasis [ref=e3339]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e3340] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-locator-option-has"
                      - paragraph [ref=e3341]:
                        - text: Narrows down the results of the method to those which contain elements matching this relative locator. For example,
                        - code [ref=e3342]: article
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e3343]: text=Playwright
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e3344]: <article><div>Playwright</div></article>
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e3345]:
                        - text: Inner locator
                        - strong [ref=e3346]: must be relative
                        - text: to the outer locator and is queried starting with the outer locator match, not the document root. For example, you can find
                        - code [ref=e3347]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e3348]: div
                        - text: in
                        - code [ref=e3349]: <article><content><div>Playwright</div></content></article>
                        - text: . However, looking for
                        - code [ref=e3350]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e3351]: article div
                        - text: will fail, because the inner locator must be relative and should not use any elements outside the
                        - code [ref=e3352]: content
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e3353]:
                        - text: Note that outer and inner locators must belong to the same frame. Inner locator must not contain
                        - link "FrameLocator" [ref=e3354] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-framelocator
                        - text: s.
                    - listitem [ref=e3355]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e3356]:
                        - code [ref=e3357]: hasNot
                        - link "Locator" [ref=e3358] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                        - emphasis [ref=e3359]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.33"
                        - link "#" [ref=e3360] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-locator-option-has-not"
                      - paragraph [ref=e3361]:
                        - text: Matches elements that do not contain an element that matches an inner locator. Inner locator is queried against the outer one. For example,
                        - code [ref=e3362]: article
                        - text: that does not have
                        - code [ref=e3363]: div
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e3364]: <article><span>Playwright</span></article>
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e3365]:
                        - text: Note that outer and inner locators must belong to the same frame. Inner locator must not contain
                        - link "FrameLocator" [ref=e3366] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-framelocator
                        - text: s.
                    - listitem [ref=e3367]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e3368]:
                        - code [ref=e3369]: hasNotText
                        - link "string" [ref=e3370] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: "|"
                        - link "RegExp" [ref=e3371] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/RegExp
                        - emphasis [ref=e3372]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.33"
                        - link "#" [ref=e3373] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-locator-option-has-not-text"
                      - paragraph [ref=e3374]:
                        - text: Matches elements that do not contain specified text somewhere inside, possibly in a child or a descendant element. When passed a
                        - link "string" [ref=e3375] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: ", matching is case-insensitive and searches for a substring."
                    - listitem [ref=e3376]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e3377]:
                        - code [ref=e3378]: hasText
                        - link "string" [ref=e3379] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: "|"
                        - link "RegExp" [ref=e3380] [cursor=pointer]:

                        - emphasis [ref=e3381]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e3382] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-locator-option-has-text"
                      - paragraph [ref=e3383]:
                        - text: Matches elements containing specified text somewhere inside, possibly in a child or a descendant element. When passed a
                        - link "string" [ref=e3384] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: ", matching is case-insensitive and searches for a substring. For example,"
                        - code [ref=e3385]: "\"Playwright\""
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e3386]: <article><div>Playwright</div></article>
                        - text: .

              - text: "Added in: v1.33"
              - paragraph [ref=e3428]: Creates a locator matching all elements that match one or both of the two locators.
              - paragraph [ref=e3429]:
                - text: Note that when both locators match something, the resulting locator will have multiple matches, potentially causing a
                - link "locator strictness" [ref=e3430] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/locators#strictness
                - text: violation.
              - paragraph [ref=e3431]:
                - strong [ref=e3432]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e3433]: Consider a scenario where you'd like to click on a "New email" button, but sometimes a security settings dialog shows up instead. In this case, you can wait for either a "New email" button, or a dialog and act accordingly.
              - generic [ref=e3434]:
                - generic [ref=e3435]:
                  - img [ref=e3437]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e3440]:
                  - text: If both "New email" button and security dialog appear on screen, the "or" locator will match both of them, possibly throwing the
                  - link "\"strict mode violation\" error" [ref=e3441] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/locators#strictness
                  - text: . In this case, you can use
                  - link "locator.first()" [ref=e3442] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-first
                  - text: to only match one of them.
              - generic [ref=e3444]:
                - code [ref=e3446]:

                  - generic [ref=e3448]: const dialog = page.getByText('Confirm security settings');
                  - generic [ref=e3449]: await expect(newEmail.or(dialog).first()).toBeVisible();
                  - generic [ref=e3450]: if (await dialog.isVisible())

              - paragraph [ref=e3611]:
                - text: "Following modification shortcuts are also supported:"
                - code [ref=e3612]: Shift
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e3613]: Control
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e3614]: Alt
                - text: ","

                - text: ","

              - paragraph [ref=e3621]:
                - text: Holding down
                - code [ref=e3622]: Shift
                - text: will type the text that corresponds to the
                - link "key" [ref=e3623] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-press-option-key
                - text: in the upper case.
              - paragraph [ref=e3624]:
                - text: If
                - link "key" [ref=e3625] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-press-option-key
                - text: is a single character, it is case-sensitive, so the values
                - code [ref=e3626]: a
                - text: and
                - code [ref=e3627]: A
                - text: will generate different respective texts.
              - paragraph [ref=e3628]:
                - text: Shortcuts such as
                - code [ref=e3629]: "key: \"Control+o\""
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e3630]: "key: \"Control++"
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e3631]: "key: \"Control+Shift+T\""
                - text: are supported as well. When specified with the modifier, modifier is pressed and being held while the subsequent key is being pressed.

                      - paragraph [ref=e3786]:
                        - text: When set to
                        - code [ref=e3787]: "\"disabled\""
                        - text: ", stops CSS animations, CSS transitions and Web Animations. Animations get different treatment depending on their duration:"
                      - list [ref=e3788]:

                          - text: finite animations are fast-forwarded to completion, so they'll fire
                          - code [ref=e3790]: transitionend
                          - text: event.
                        - listitem [ref=e3791]: infinite animations are canceled to initial state, and then played over after the screenshot.
                      - paragraph [ref=e3792]:
                        - text: Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e3793]: "\"allow\""
                        - text: that leaves animations untouched.

                - strong [ref=e3884]: Returns
              - list [ref=e3885]:
                - listitem [ref=e3886]:
                  - link "Promise" [ref=e3887] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - link "#" [ref=e3889] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#locator-screenshot-return"
              - paragraph [ref=e3890]:
                - strong [ref=e3891]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e3892]: This method captures a screenshot of the page, clipped to the size and position of a particular element matching the locator. If the element is covered by other elements, it will not be actually visible on the screenshot. If the element is a scrollable container, only the currently scrolled content will be visible on the screenshot.
              - paragraph [ref=e3893]:
                - text: This method waits for the
                - link "actionability" [ref=e3894] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/actionability
                - text: checks, then scrolls element into view before taking a screenshot. If the element is detached from DOM, the method throws an error.
              - paragraph [ref=e3895]: Returns the buffer with the captured screenshot.
              - separator [ref=e3896]
              - heading "scrollIntoViewIfNeededDirect link to scrollIntoViewIfNeeded" [level=3] [ref=e3897]:
                - text: scrollIntoViewIfNeeded
                - link "Direct link to scrollIntoViewIfNeeded" [ref=e3898] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#locator-scroll-into-view-if-needed"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.14"
              - paragraph [ref=e3899]:
                - text: This method waits for
                - link "actionability" [ref=e3900] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/actionability
                - text: checks, then tries to scroll element into view, unless it is completely visible as defined by
                - link "IntersectionObserver" [ref=e3901] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Intersection_Observer_API
                - text: "'s"
                - code [ref=e3902]: ratio
                - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e3903]:
                - text: See
                - link "scrolling" [ref=e3904] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/input#scrolling
                - text: for alternative ways to scroll.

                      - paragraph [ref=e4012]:

                        - link "string" [ref=e4014] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e4015]: (optional)

                    - listitem [ref=e4018]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e4019]:
                        - code [ref=e4020]: index
                        - link "number" [ref=e4021] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Number_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e4022]: (optional)
                      - paragraph [ref=e4023]: Matches by the index. Optional.
                  - paragraph [ref=e4024]:
                    - text: Options to select. If the
                    - code [ref=e4025]: <select>
                    - text: has the
                    - code [ref=e4026]: multiple
                    - text: attribute, all matching options are selected, otherwise only the first option matching one of the passed options is selected. String values are matching both values and labels. Option is considered matching if all specified properties match.
                - listitem [ref=e4027]:

                - code [ref=e4079]: <select>

                - text: If the target element is not a
                - code [ref=e4081]: <select>
                - text: element, this method throws an error. However, if the element is inside the
                - code [ref=e4082]: <label>

                - link "control" [ref=e4083] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLLabelElement/control
                - text: ", the control will be used instead."
              - paragraph [ref=e4084]: Returns the array of option values that have been successfully selected.

                - code [ref=e4087]: input

              - paragraph [ref=e4245]:
                - strong [ref=e4246]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e4247]: "This method checks or unchecks an element by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e4248]:
                - listitem [ref=e4249]: Ensure that matched element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws.
                - listitem [ref=e4250]: If the element already has the right checked state, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e4251]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e4252] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e4253] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-set-checked-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e4254]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e4255]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e4256] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e4257]: Ensure that the element is now checked or unchecked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e4258]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e4259] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-set-checked-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e4260] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

                - text: Sets the value of the file input to these file paths or files. If some of the
                - code [ref=e4368]: filePaths
                - text: are relative paths, then they are resolved relative to the current working directory. For empty array, clears the selected files.

                  - text: option is set.

                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.touchscreen" [ref=e4486] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-touchscreen

                  - link "position" [ref=e4487] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-tap-option-position
                  - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e4488]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e4489]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e4490] [cursor=pointer]:

                - text: ", this method throws a"

                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

              - list [ref=e4653]:
                - listitem [ref=e4654]: Ensure that element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws. If the element is already unchecked, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e4655]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e4656] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - text: option is set.

                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e4661]: Ensure that the element is now unchecked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e4662]: If the element is detached from the DOM at any moment during the action, this method throws.

                - link "state" [ref=e4670] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-wait-for-option-state
                - text: option.
              - paragraph [ref=e4671]:
                - text: If target element already satisfies the condition, the method returns immediately. Otherwise, waits for up to
                - link "timeout" [ref=e4672] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-wait-for-option-timeout
                - text: milliseconds until the condition is met.

                - listitem [ref=e4691]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e4694]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e4695]:
                    - listitem [ref=e4696]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e4697]:
                        - code [ref=e4698]: state
                        - text: "\"attached\" | \"detached\" | \"visible\" | \"hidden\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e4699]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e4700] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-wait-for-option-state"
                      - paragraph [ref=e4701]:
                        - text: Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e4702]: "'visible'"
                        - text: ". Can be either:"
                      - list [ref=e4703]:
                        - listitem [ref=e4704]:
                          - code [ref=e4705]: "'attached'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to be present in DOM."
                        - listitem [ref=e4706]:
                          - code [ref=e4707]: "'detached'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to not be present in DOM."
                        - listitem [ref=e4708]:
                          - code [ref=e4709]: "'visible'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to have non-empty bounding box and no"
                          - code [ref=e4710]: visibility:hidden
                          - text: . Note that element without any content or with
                          - code [ref=e4711]: display:none
                          - text: has an empty bounding box and is not considered visible.
                        - listitem [ref=e4712]:
                          - code [ref=e4713]: "'hidden'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to be either detached from DOM, or have an empty bounding box or"
                          - code [ref=e4714]: visibility:hidden
                          - text: . This is opposite to the
                          - code [ref=e4715]: "'visible'"
                          - text: option.
                    - listitem [ref=e4716]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e4717]:
                        - code [ref=e4718]: timeout
                        - link "number" [ref=e4719] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Number_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e4720]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e4721] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#locator-wait-for-option-timeout"
                      - paragraph [ref=e4722]:
                        - text: Maximum time in milliseconds. Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e4723]: "0"
                        - text: "- no timeout. The default value can be changed via"
                        - code [ref=e4724]: actionTimeout
                        - text: option in the config, or by using the
                        - link "browserContext.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e4725] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-set-default-timeout
                        - text: or
                        - link "page.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e4726] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-default-timeout
                        - text: methods.
